on persistence_changed
	set_background_animation(CC[1]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	call set_key_colors{UserDefined, None}
	call keyswitches_color_keys{UserDefined, None}
	subarticulation_purge(0, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	subarticulation_purge(9, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	subarticulation_purge(10, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	subarticulation_purge(12, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	subarticulation_purge(15, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	subarticulation_purge(21, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end on

on note
	ignore_event(EVENT_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE{unknown}, 1){Builtin, None}
	keyswitches_on_note(EVENT_NOTE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	if(pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} = - 1)
		pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}
		last_pressed[EVENT_NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}
		key_velocity[EVENT_NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} := EVENT_VELOCITY{unknown}
		inc(num_pressed_keys{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end if
	last_on_note_callback{unknown} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{unknown}
	wait_or_zero(note_selection_time{unknown} * 1000){UserDefined, None}
	if(last_on_note_callback{unknown} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{unknown})
		update_selected_notes{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end on

on release
	if(get_event_mark(EVENT_ID{unknown}, MARK_1{unknown}){Builtin, None} = FALSE{unknown})
		set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None}
		last_release_callback{unknown} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{unknown}
		ignore_event(EVENT_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		pressed_keys[EVENT_NOTE{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
		dec(num_pressed_keys{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(sustain_pedal{unknown} = OFF{unknown})
			articulations_note_off(0, EVENT_NOTE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			wait_or_zero(note_selection_time{unknown} * 1000){UserDefined, None}
			if(last_release_callback{unknown} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{unknown})
				update_selected_notes{UserDefined, None}
			end if
		end if
	end if
end on

on controller
	ignore_controller{Builtin, None}
	declare local controller_value : int := CC[CC_NUM{unknown}]{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	if(CC_NUM{unknown} = 1)
		buffer_modwheel_animation(CC[1]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		sli_modwheel_slider{unknown} -> value := CC[1]{unknown}
	end if
	if(CC_NUM{unknown} = 64)
		if(CC[64]{unknown} > 63)
			sustain_pedal_actual{unknown} := ON{unknown}
		else
			sustain_pedal_actual{unknown} := OFF{unknown}
			sustain_pedal{unknown} := OFF{unknown}
			for i{unknown} := 0 to 127
				if(pressed_keys[i{unknown}]{unknown} = - 1)
					for ii{unknown} := 0 to NUM_INSTRUMENTS0{unknown} - 1
						articulations_note_off(ii{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					end for
				end if
			end for
		end if
	end if
	wait_or_zero(lookahead{unknown} * 1000){UserDefined, None}
	sustain_pedal{unknown} := sustain_pedal_actual{unknown}
	if(CC_NUM{unknown} = 1)
		set_modulation_position(0, controller_value{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		call cc_on_controller{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end on

on poly_at

end on

	call delay_buffer_execute{UserDefined, None}

	if((animation_frame_counter{unknown} = 0) and (next_modwheel_animation_frame{unknown} # - 1))
		set_background_animation(next_modwheel_animation_frame{unknown}){UserDefined, None}

			editor_update_modwheel_position(next_modwheel_animation_frame{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		end if
		next_modwheel_animation_frame{unknown} := - 1
	end if
	animation_frame_counter{unknown} := (animation_frame_counter{unknown} + 1) mod (ANIMATION_RESOLUTION{unknown} / LISTENER_RESOLUTION{unknown})
end on

on ui_control(xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown})
	xy_modwheel_assignment[0 + 1]{unknown} := 1
	xy_modwheel_assignment[4 + 1]{unknown} := 1
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{unknown} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{unknown})
		if((xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> active_index = 0) or (xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> active_index = 4))
			lbl_fade_circle_md{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		end if
	else
		if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{unknown} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_UP{unknown})
			lbl_fade_circle_md{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
		end if
	end if
	ma_cb_id{unknown} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{unknown}
	if((xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> active_index = 2) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown}))
		if(xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} < xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown})
			xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} := xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown}
		end if
		loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := int(xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown} * 127){Builtin, None}
	else
		if(((xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> active_index = 0) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown})) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown}))
			lbl_fade_circle_md{unknown} -> x := xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> x + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} * real(xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> width - 20){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
			loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := int(round((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown}) * 127){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(((xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> active_index = 4) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown})) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown}))
				lbl_fade_circle_md{unknown} -> x := xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> x + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown} * real(xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> width - 20){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
				loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := int((xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown} - xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown}) * 127){Builtin, None}
			else
				if((xy_modwheel_assignment{unknown} -> active_index = 6) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown}))
					if(xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown} > xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown})
						xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown} := xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown}
					end if
					loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := int(xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown} * 127){Builtin, None}
				end if
			end if
		end if
	end if
	wait(10000){Builtin, None}
	if(ma_cb_id{unknown} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{unknown})
		call update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, None}
		call update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end on

on ui_control(xy_center_circles{unknown})
	cc_cb_id{unknown} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{unknown}
	declare local angle : real {Reuses: 0}
	declare local value : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local distance : real {Reuses: 0}
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{unknown} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{unknown})
		distance{unknown} := center_circle_distance(xy_center_circles[0]{unknown}, xy_center_circles[1]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		angle{unknown} := center_circle_angle(xy_center_circles[0]{unknown}, xy_center_circles[1]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		value{unknown} := angle_to_value(angle{unknown}, 0.7, (NI_MATH_PI{unknown} * 2) - 0.7){UserDefined, None}
		if((distance{unknown} >= 0.32) and (distance{unknown} < 0.36))
			selected_subarticulation{unknown} := 0
		else
			if((distance{unknown} >= 0.36) and (distance{unknown} < 0.4))
				selected_subarticulation{unknown} := 1
			else
				if((distance{unknown} >= 0.4) and (distance{unknown} < 0.44))
					selected_subarticulation{unknown} := 2
				else
					if((distance{unknown} >= 0.44) and (distance{unknown} < 0.48))
						selected_subarticulation{unknown} := 3
					end if
				end if
			end if
		end if
		if(abs(value{unknown} - loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} < 10)
			selected_circle_end{unknown} := 0
		else
			if(abs(value{unknown} - loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} < 10)
				selected_circle_end{unknown} := 1
			else
				selected_circle_end{unknown} := - 1
			end if
		end if
		call update_subarticulation_selection{UserDefined, None}
	end if
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{unknown} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG{unknown})
		wait(10000){Builtin, None}
		if((cc_cb_id{unknown} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{unknown}) and (selected_circle_end{unknown} # - 1))
			angle{unknown} := center_circle_angle(xy_center_circles[0]{unknown}, xy_center_circles[1]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			value{unknown} := angle_to_value(angle{unknown}, 0.7, (NI_MATH_PI{unknown} * 2) - 0.7){UserDefined, None}
			if(selected_circle_end{unknown} = 0)
				if(value{unknown} < ((loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} - loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}) - loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}))
					loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := value{unknown}
				end if
			else
				if(selected_circle_end{unknown} = 1)
					if(value{unknown} > ((loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} + loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}) + loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}))
						loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := value{unknown}
					end if
				end if
			end if
			call update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, None}
			call update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, None}
		end if
	end if
end on

function sh_right_safe(val : unknown, pos : unknown)
	return ((sh_right(val{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None} .and. (1 * sh_left(1, 31 - pos{unknown}){Builtin, None})) .or. sh_right(val{unknown} .and. 2147483647, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function is_in_range(value : unknown, a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (1 + (sh_right(b{unknown} - value{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(value{unknown} - a{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function swap(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	a{unknown} := a{unknown} .xor. b{unknown}
	b{unknown} := b{unknown} .xor. a{unknown}
	a{unknown} := a{unknown} .xor. b{unknown}
end function

function gt(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (- sh_right(b{unknown} - a{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function ge(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (sh_right(a{unknown} - b{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None} + 1)
end function

function eq(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (- sh_right(abs(a{unknown} - b{unknown}){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function lt(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (- sh_right(a{unknown} - b{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function le(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (1 + sh_right(b{unknown} - a{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function ne(x : unknown)
	return (abs(sh_right(abs(x{unknown}){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function neg(x : unknown)
	return (- sh_right(x{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function bool(x : unknown)
	return (1 + sh_right(abs(x{unknown}){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function sign(x : unknown)
	return (sh_right(x{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. 1)
end function

function sign3(x : unknown)
	return (sign(x{unknown}){UserDefined, None} .and. - bool(x{unknown}){UserDefined, None})
end function

function bitlist.load(bit_list : unknown, val : unknown)
	bit_list{unknown} := val{unknown}
end function

function bitlist.clear(bit_list : unknown)
	bit_list{unknown} := 0
end function

function bitlist.control_to_bitlist(bit_list : unknown, ui_array : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to min(31, num_elements[ui_array{unknown}] - 1){UserDefined, None}
		bitlist.set(bit_list{unknown}, lib.i{unknown}, ui_array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} -> value){UserDefined, None}
	end for
end function

function bitlist.bitlist_to_control(bit_list : unknown, ui_array : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to min(31, num_elements[ui_array{unknown}] - 1){UserDefined, None}
		set_control_par(ui_array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, bitlist.get(bit_list{unknown}, lib.i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function bitlist.set(bit_list : unknown, idx : unknown, val : unknown)
	bit_list{unknown} := .not. (.not. ((bit_list{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, 31 - idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. .not. ((bit_list{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, 31 - idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. (- val{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, 31 - idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}))) .and. .not. ((- val{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, 31 - idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. .not. ((bit_list{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, 31 - idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. (- val{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, 31 - idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}))))
end function

function bitlist.set_range(bit_list : unknown, start_idx : unknown, end_idx : unknown, val : unknown)
	bit_list{unknown} := (eq(val{unknown}, 1){UserDefined, None} * ((eq(end_idx{unknown} - start_idx{unknown}, 32){UserDefined, None} * sh_right(- 1, 32){Builtin, None}) + (bit_list{unknown} .or. sh_left(.not. sh_left(- 1, end_idx{unknown} - start_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 32 - end_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}))) + (eq(val{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} * (lt(end_idx{unknown} - start_idx{unknown}, 32){UserDefined, None} * (bit_list{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(.not. sh_left(- 1, end_idx{unknown} - start_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 32 - end_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None})))
end function

function bitlist.get(bit_list : unknown, idx : unknown)
	return (sh_right(bit_list{unknown}, 31 - idx{unknown}){Builtin, None} .and. 1)
end function

function bitlist.get_range(bit_list : unknown, start_idx : unknown, end_idx : unknown)
	return ((eq(end_idx{unknown} - start_idx{unknown}, 32){UserDefined, None} * bit_list{unknown}) + sh_left(sh_right(bit_list{unknown}, 32 - end_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None} .and. .not. sh_left(- 1, end_idx{unknown} - start_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}, 32 - end_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function bitlist.reverse(bit_list : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to 32 / 2
		bitlist.swap(bit_list{unknown}, lib.i{unknown}, 31 - lib.i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end for
end function

function bitlist.swap(bit_list : unknown, idx1 : unknown, idx2 : unknown)
	declare local val_idx1 : unknown := bitlist.get(bit_list{unknown}, idx1{unknown}){UserDefined, None} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local val_idx2 : unknown := bitlist.get(bit_list{unknown}, idx2{unknown}){UserDefined, None} {Reuses: 0}
	bitlist.set(bit_list{unknown}, idx1{unknown}, val_idx2{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	bitlist.set(bit_list{unknown}, idx2{unknown}, val_idx1{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function bitlist.print(bit_list : unknown)
	declare local bl : string := "[" {Reuses: 0}
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to 32 - 1
		bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & bitlist.get(bit_list{unknown}, lib.i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		if(lib.i{unknown} < (32 - 1))
			bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & ", "
		end if
	end for
	bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & "]"
	message(bl{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function vector.push_back(ls : unknown, val : unknown)
	ls[max(1, ls[0]{unknown} + 1){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} := val{unknown}
	inc(ls[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function vector.clear(ls : unknown)
	ls[0]{unknown} := 0
end function

function vector.set(ls : unknown, idx : unknown, val : unknown)
	ls[min(ls[0]{unknown} + 1, idx{unknown} + 1){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} := val{unknown}
	if(idx{unknown} > ls[0]{unknown})
		inc(ls[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function vector.insert(ls : unknown, idx : unknown, val : unknown)
	if(idx{unknown} > ls[0]{unknown})
		vector.push_back(ls{unknown}, val{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	else
		for lib.i{unknown} := ls[0]{unknown} downto idx{unknown} + 1
			ls[lib.i{unknown} + 1]{unknown} := ls[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
		end for
		ls[idx{unknown} + 1]{unknown} := val{unknown}
		inc(ls[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function vector.combine(ls : unknown, ls2 : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to ls2[0]{unknown} - 1
		vector.push_back(ls{unknown}, ls2[min(ls2[0]{unknown} + 1, lib.i{unknown} + 1){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end for
end function

function vector.erase(ls : unknown, idx : unknown)
	if(idx{unknown} < ls[0]{unknown})
		for lib.i{unknown} := idx{unknown} + 2 to ls[0]{unknown}
			ls[lib.i{unknown} - 1]{unknown} := ls[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
		end for
	end if
	dec(ls[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function vector.pop_back(ls : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := ls[ls[0]{unknown}]{unknown}
	dec(ls[0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function vector.print(ls : unknown)
	declare local l : string := "[" {Reuses: 0}
	for lib.i{unknown} := 1 to ls[0]{unknown}
		l{unknown} := l{unknown} & ls[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
		if(lib.i{unknown} < ls[0]{unknown})
			l{unknown} := l{unknown} & ", "
		end if
	end for
	l{unknown} := l{unknown} & "]"
	message(l{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function vector.search(ls : unknown, value : unknown)
	return (search[ls{unknown}, value{unknown}, 1, ls[0]{unknown}])
end function

function vector.to_table(vec : unknown, tbl : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to min(vec[0]{unknown} + 1, get_menu_item_value(tbl{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} + 1){UserDefined, None} - 1
		set_menu_item_value(tbl{unknown}, lib.i{unknown}, vec[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function tinylist.print(ls : unknown)
	declare local bl : string := "[" {Reuses: 0}
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to (31 / ((ls{unknown} .and. 3) + 2)) - 1

		if(lib.i{unknown} < ((31 / ((ls{unknown} .and. 3) + 2)) - 1))
			bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & ", "
		end if
	end for
	bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & "]"
	message(bl{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function tinylist2d.get(ls : unknown, x : unknown, y : unknown)
	return (tinylist.get(ls[x{unknown}]{unknown}, y{unknown}){UserDefined, None})

	return (tinylist.search(ls[row{unknown}]{unknown}, val{unknown}){UserDefined, None})
end function

function tinylist2d.print(ls : unknown)
	declare local bl : string {Reuses: 0}
	for lib.ii{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[ls{unknown}] - 1
		bl{unknown} := lib.ii{unknown} & ": ["
		for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to (31 / ((ls[lib.ii{unknown}]{unknown} .and. 3) + 2)) - 1

			if(lib.i{unknown} < ((31 / ((ls[lib.ii{unknown}]{unknown} .and. 3) + 2)) - 1))
				bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & ", "
			end if
		end for
		bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & "]"
		message(bl{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function table.set(ls : unknown, idx : unknown, val : unknown)
	set_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, min(get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} + 1, idx{unknown} + 1){UserDefined, None}, val{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	if(idx{unknown} > get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None})
		set_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0, get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} + 1){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function table.get(ls : unknown, idx : unknown)
	return (get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, min(get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} + 1, idx{unknown} + 1){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function table.push_back(ls : unknown, val : unknown)
	set_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, max(get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} + 1, 1){UserDefined, None}, val{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	set_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0, get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} + 1){Builtin, None}
end function

function table.to_vector(tbl : unknown, vec : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to min(vec[0]{unknown} + 1, get_menu_item_value(tbl{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} + 1){UserDefined, None} - 1
		vec[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} := get_menu_item_value(tbl{unknown}, lib.i{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function table.print(ls : unknown)
	declare local l : string := "[" {Reuses: 0}
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} - 1
		l{unknown} := l{unknown} & table.get(ls{unknown}, lib.i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		if(lib.i{unknown} < (get_menu_item_value(ls{unknown}, 0){Builtin, None} - 1))
			l{unknown} := l{unknown} & ", "
		end if
	end for
	l{unknown} := l{unknown} & "]"
	message(l{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function array.remove(array : unknown, idx : unknown)
	lib.ii{unknown} := 0
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[array{unknown}] - 1
		if(lib.i{unknown} # idx{unknown})
			array[lib.ii{unknown}]{unknown} := array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
			inc(lib.ii{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
end function

function array.clear(array : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[array{unknown}] - 1
		array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} := 0
	end for
end function

function array.reset(array : unknown, val : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[array{unknown}] - 1
		array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} := val{unknown}
	end for
end function

function array.max(array : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := array[0]{unknown}
	for lib.i{unknown} := 1 to num_elements[array{unknown}] - 1
		result{unknown} := max(array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}, result{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end for
end function

function array.min(array : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := array[0]{unknown}
	for lib.i{unknown} := 1 to num_elements[array{unknown}] - 1
		result{unknown} := min(array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}, result{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end for
end function

function array.map(array : unknown, func : unknown) -> result : unknown
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[array{unknown}] - 1
		array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} := func(array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}){Undefined, None}
	end for
end function

function array.reduce(array : unknown, func : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := array[0]{unknown}
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[array{unknown}] - 1
		result{unknown} := func(result{unknown}, array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}){Undefined, None}
	end for
end function

function array.copy(original : unknown, empty : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[original{unknown}] - 1
		empty[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} := original[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
	end for
end function

function array.cumsum(array : unknown, new_array : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[array{unknown}] - 1
		new_array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} := new_array[max(0, lib.i{unknown} - 1){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} + array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
	end for
end function

function array.insert(array : unknown, idx : unknown, val : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := num_elements[array{unknown}] - 2 downto idx{unknown}
		array[lib.i{unknown} + 1]{unknown} := array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}
	end for
	array[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := val{unknown}
end function

function ui_array.map(control_array : unknown, param : unknown, val : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[control_array{unknown}] - 1
		set_control_par(control_array[lib.i{unknown}]{unknown}, param{unknown}, val{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function ui_array.toggle_button(control_array : unknown, exception_idx : unknown)
	ui_array.map(control_array{unknown}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None}
	control_array[clamp(exception_idx{unknown}, 0, num_elements[control_array{unknown}] - 1){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} -> value := 1
end function

.and. 1431655765)) .and. 858993459) + (sh_right((float_mask[1]{unknown} .and. 1431655765) + (sh_right(float_mask[1]{unknown}, 1){Builtin, None} .and. 1431655765), 2){Builtin, None} .and. 858993459), 4){Builtin, None} .and. 252645135), 8){Builtin, None} .and. 16711935), 16){Builtin, None} .and. 65535)) - (eq(val{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} * 32)){Builtin, None})
end function

function floatmask.set(float_mask : unknown, idx : unknown, val : unknown)
	float_mask[idx{unknown} / 32]{unknown} := (float_mask[idx{unknown} / 32]{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, (31 - idx{unknown}) mod 32){Builtin, None}) .or. sh_left(val{unknown}, (31 - idx{unknown}) mod 32){Builtin, None}
end function

function floatmask.set_range(float_mask : unknown, start_idx : unknown, end_idx : unknown, val : unknown)
	bitlist.set_range(float_mask[0]{unknown}, min(32, start_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, min(32, end_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, val{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	bitlist.set_range(float_mask[1]{unknown}, max(32, start_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - 32, max(32, end_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - 32, val{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function floatmask.get(float_mask : unknown, idx : unknown)
	return (sh_right(float_mask[idx{unknown} / 32]{unknown}, (31 - idx{unknown}) mod 32){Builtin, None} .and. 1)
end function

function floatmask.get_range(float_mask : unknown, start_idx : unknown, end_idx : unknown, return_mask : unknown)
	return_mask[0]{unknown} := bitlist.get_range(float_mask[0]{unknown}, min(32, start_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, min(32, end_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}
	return_mask[1]{unknown} := bitlist.get_range(float_mask[1]{unknown}, max(32, start_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - 32, max(32, end_idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - 32){UserDefined, None}
end function

function floatmask.print(float_mask : unknown)
	declare local bl : string := "[" {Reuses: 0}
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to 64 - 1
		bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & floatmask.get(float_mask{unknown}, lib.i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		if(lib.i{unknown} < (64 - 1))
			bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & ", "
		end if
	end for
	bl{unknown} := bl{unknown} & "]"
	message(bl{unknown}){Builtin, None}
end function

function floatmask.sh_left(float_mask : unknown, pos : unknown)
	if(pos{unknown} < 32)
		float_mask[0]{unknown} := sh_left(float_mask[0]{unknown}, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right_safe(float_mask[1]{unknown}, 32 - pos{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		float_mask[1]{unknown} := sh_left(float_mask[1]{unknown}, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	else
		float_mask[0]{unknown} := sh_left(float_mask[1]{unknown}, pos{unknown} - 32){Builtin, None}
		float_mask[1]{unknown} := 0
	end if
end function

function floatmask.sh_right(float_mask : unknown, pos : unknown)
	if(pos{unknown} < 32)
		float_mask[1]{unknown} := sh_right_safe(float_mask[1]{unknown}, pos{unknown}){UserDefined, None} .or. sh_left(float_mask[0]{unknown}, 32 - pos{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		float_mask[0]{unknown} := sh_right_safe(float_mask[0]{unknown}, pos{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	else
		float_mask[1]{unknown} := sh_right_safe(float_mask[0]{unknown}, pos{unknown} - 32){UserDefined, None}
		float_mask[0]{unknown} := 0
	end if
end function

function floatmask.and(float_mask1 : unknown, float_mask2 : unknown, return_mask : unknown)
	return_mask[0]{unknown} := float_mask1[0]{unknown} .and. float_mask2[0]{unknown}
	return_mask[1]{unknown} := float_mask1[1]{unknown} .and. float_mask2[1]{unknown}
end function

function floatmask.or(float_mask1 : unknown, float_mask2 : unknown, return_mask : unknown)
	return_mask[0]{unknown} := float_mask1[0]{unknown} .or. float_mask2[0]{unknown}
	return_mask[1]{unknown} := float_mask1[1]{unknown} .or. float_mask2[1]{unknown}
end function

function floatmask.not(float_mask : unknown, return_mask : unknown)
	return_mask[0]{unknown} := .not. float_mask[0]{unknown}
	return_mask[1]{unknown} := .not. float_mask[1]{unknown}
end function

function floatmask.equal(float_mask1 : unknown, float_mask2 : unknown)
	return (eq(((float_mask1[0]{unknown} - float_mask2[0]{unknown}) + float_mask1[1]{unknown}) - float_mask2[1]{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None})
end function

function floatmask.is_empty(float_mask : unknown)
	return (ne(bool(float_mask[0]{unknown} + float_mask[1]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None})
end function

function assert(func : unknown, expected : unknown)
	declare local result : unknown {Reuses: 0}
	if((tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}) = 0)
		_test_init_message(tests.separator{string}){UserDefined, None}
		tests.time_init{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	end if
	tests.time_elapsed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	result{unknown} := func{unknown}
	tests.time_elapsed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown} - tests.time_elapsed{unknown}
	tests.time_end{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	if(result{unknown} = expected{unknown})
		inc(tests.counter_successful{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_successful(tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, result{unknown}, expected{unknown}, tests.time_elapsed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	else
		inc(tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_unsuccessful(tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, result{unknown}, expected{unknown}, tests.time_elapsed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function assert_summary
	declare local success_rate : real {Reuses: 0}
	success_rate{unknown} := (int_to_real(tests.counter_successful{unknown}){Builtin, None} / int_to_real(tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}){Builtin, None}) * 100
	_tests_summary_message(tests.separator{string}, tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, tests.time_init{unknown}, tests.time_end{unknown}, success_rate{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function assert_side_effects(func : unknown, variable : unknown, expected : unknown)
	if((stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}) = 0)
		_test_init_message(stests.separator{string}){UserDefined, None}
		stests.time_init{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	end if
	stests.time_elapsed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	func{Undefined, None}
	stests.time_elapsed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown} - stests.time_elapsed{unknown}
	stests.time_end{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
	if(variable{unknown} = expected{unknown})
		inc(stests.counter_successful{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_successful(stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, variable{unknown}, expected{unknown}, stests.time_elapsed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	else
		inc(stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_unsuccessful(stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, variable{unknown}, expected{unknown}, stests.time_elapsed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function assert_side_effects_summary
	declare local success_rate : real {Reuses: 0}
	success_rate{unknown} := (int_to_real(stests.counter_successful{unknown}){Builtin, None} / int_to_real(stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}){Builtin, None}) * 100
	_tests_summary_message(stests.separator{string}, stests.counter_successful{unknown} + stests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}, stests.time_init{unknown}, stests.time_end{unknown}, success_rate{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function _test_init_message(separator : unknown)
	message("RUN TESTS"){Builtin, None}
end function

function _test_message_successful(count : unknown, got : unknown, expected : unknown, time_elapsed : unknown)
	message("Test " & count{unknown} & " SUCCEEDED Ran for " & time_elapsed{unknown} & " ms."){Builtin, None}
end function

function _test_message_unsuccessful(count : unknown, got : unknown, expected : unknown, time_elapsed : unknown)
	message("Test " & count{unknown} & " FAILED. Got " & got{unknown} & ", expected " & expected{unknown} & "." & " Ran for " & time_elapsed{unknown} & " ms."){Builtin, None}
end function

function _tests_summary_message(separator : unknown, count : unknown, time_start : unknown, time_end : unknown, success_rate : unknown)
	message(separator{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	message("TESTS SUMMARY"){Builtin, None}
	message("Ran " & count{unknown} & " tests in " & (time_end{unknown} - time_start{unknown}) & " ms."){Builtin, None}
	message(success_rate{unknown} & "% Success, " & tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown} & " out of " & (tests.counter_successful{unknown} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{unknown}) & " tests failed."){Builtin, None}
end function

function scale.range(input : unknown, currentMin : unknown, currentMax : unknown, scaleToMin : unknown, scaleToMax : unknown)
	return ((((input{unknown} - currentMin{unknown}) * (scaleToMax{unknown} - scaleToMin{unknown})) / (currentMax{unknown} - currentMin{unknown})) + scaleToMin{unknown})
end function

function scale.range.real(input : unknown, currentMin : unknown, currentMax : unknown, scaleToMin : unknown, scaleToMax : unknown)
	return (real_to_int((((int_to_real(input{unknown}){Builtin, None} - currentMin{unknown}) * (scaleToMax{unknown} - scaleToMin{unknown})) / (currentMax{unknown} - currentMin{unknown})) + scaleToMin{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.range.slider(input : unknown, scaleToMin : unknown, scaleToMax : unknown)
	return (real_to_int(((input{unknown} * (scaleToMax{unknown} - scaleToMin{unknown})) / 1e+06) + scaleToMin{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.slider(input : unknown, scaleToMin : unknown, scaleToMax : unknown)
	return (real_to_int(((int_to_real(input{unknown}){Builtin, None} * (scaleToMax{unknown} - scaleToMin{unknown})) / 1e+06) + scaleToMin{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.range.log(input : unknown, currentMin : unknown, currentMax : unknown, scaleToMin : unknown, scaleToMax : unknown)
	return (pow(10, (log(scaleToMin{unknown}){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None}) + (((input{unknown} - currentMin{unknown}) / (currentMax{unknown} - currentMin{unknown})) * ((log(scaleToMax{unknown}){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None}) - (log(scaleToMin{unknown}){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None})))){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.clamp.to(input : unknown, fromMin : unknown, fromMax : unknown, toMin : unknown, toMax : unknown)
	return (real_to_int(scale.range(int_to_real(((input{unknown} * (1 + (sh_right(fromMax{unknown} - input{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(input{unknown} - fromMin{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))) - (fromMin{unknown} * sh_right(input{unknown} - fromMin{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})) - (fromMax{unknown} * sh_right(fromMax{unknown} - input{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(fromMin{unknown}){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(fromMax{unknown}){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(toMin{unknown}){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(toMax{unknown}){Builtin, None}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function isBitSet(x : unknown, pos : unknown)
	return (sh_right(x{unknown}, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None} .and. 1)
end function

function set_bit(x : unknown, pos : unknown)
	return (x{unknown} .or. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function clear_bit(x : unknown, pos : unknown)
	return (x{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function flip_bit(x : unknown, pos : unknown)
	return (.not. (.not. (x{unknown} .and. .not. (x{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None})) .and. .not. (sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None} .and. .not. (x{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None}))))
end function

function modify_bit(x : unknown, pos : unknown, state : unknown)
	return (.not. (.not. ((x{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. .not. ((x{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. (- state{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None}))) .and. .not. ((- state{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. .not. ((x{unknown} .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None}) .and. (- state{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, pos{unknown}){Builtin, None})))))
end function

function decimal.to.binary(input : unknown, output_array : unknown)
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[output_array{unknown}] - 2
		output_array[(num_elements[output_array{unknown}] - 2) - lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} := abs(sh_right(- (input{unknown} .and. sh_left(1, lib.i{unknown}){Builtin, None}), 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function binary.to.decimal(length : unknown, input_array : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := 0
	for lib.i{unknown} := 0 to length{unknown} - 1
		result{unknown} := result{unknown} + (input_array[(length{unknown} - 1) - lib.i{unknown}]{unknown} * real_to_int(pow(2, int_to_real(lib.i{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
	end for
end function

function clamp(x : unknown, min : unknown, max : unknown)
	return (((x{unknown} * is_in_range(x{unknown}, min{unknown}, max{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) - (min{unknown} * sh_right(x{unknown} - min{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None})) - (max{unknown} * sh_right(max{unknown} - x{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function clamp.slider(x : unknown)
	return ((x{unknown} * is_in_range(x{unknown}, 0, 1000000){UserDefined, None}) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - x{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function clip(x : unknown, top : unknown)
	return ((x{unknown} * is_in_range(x{unknown}, 0, top{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) - (top{unknown} * sh_right(top{unknown} - x{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function max(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (a{unknown} - ((a{unknown} - b{unknown}) .and. sh_right(a{unknown} - b{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function max4(a : unknown, b : unknown, c : unknown, d : unknown)
	return (max(a{unknown}, b{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - ((max(a{unknown}, b{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - max(c{unknown}, d{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) .and. sh_right(max(a{unknown}, b{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - max(c{unknown}, d{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function min(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (a{unknown} - ((a{unknown} - b{unknown}) .and. sh_right(b{unknown} - a{unknown}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function min4(a : unknown, b : unknown, c : unknown, d : unknown)
	return (min(a{unknown}, b{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - ((min(a{unknown}, b{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - min(c{unknown}, d{unknown}){UserDefined, None}) .and. sh_right(min(c{unknown}, d{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - min(a{unknown}, b{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function div(x : unknown, y : unknown)
	return ((x{unknown} + (x{unknown} mod y{unknown})) / y{unknown})
end function

function log(base : unknown, value : unknown)
	return (log(value{unknown}){Builtin, None} / log(int_to_real(base{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function decimals(value : unknown, div : unknown, dec_div : unknown)
	return ((value{unknown} / div{unknown}) & '.' & abs((value{unknown} mod div{unknown}) / dec_div{unknown}){Builtin, None})
end function

function fmod(a : unknown, b : unknown)
	return (a{unknown} - (floor(a{unknown} / b{unknown}){Builtin, None} * b{unknown}))
end function

function trim(input : unknown, decim : unknown)
	return (round(input{unknown} * pow(10, int_to_real(decim{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / pow(10, int_to_real(decim{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function non_rpt_random(last_random : unknown, min_random : unknown, max_random : unknown) -> result : unknown
	result{unknown} := Rand(min_random{unknown} + 1, max_random{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	result{unknown} := (last_random{unknown} + result{unknown}) mod (max_random{unknown} + 1)
	last_random{unknown} := result{unknown}
end function

function Rand(min : unknown, max : unknown) -> result : unknown
	___M.Seed{unknown} := (8088405 * ___M.Seed{unknown}) + 1
	result{unknown} := ((sh_right(___M.Seed{unknown}, 8){Builtin, None} .and. 16777215) mod ((max{unknown} - min{unknown}) + 1)) + min{unknown}
end function

function RandomSeed
	___M.Seed{unknown} := KSP_TIMER{unknown}
end function

function ResetRand
	___M.Seed{unknown} := 1107155288
end function

function note_to_string(instrument : int, note : int)
	declare local reduced_note : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local string : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	if((instrument{unknown} = INSTRUMENT_TYPE_VIOLIN_1{unknown}) or (instrument{unknown} = INSTRUMENT_TYPE_VIOLIN_2{unknown}))
		reduced_note{unknown} := (note{unknown} - 55) - mnu_finger_position{unknown}
		if(reduced_note{unknown} >= 0)
			string{unknown} := reduced_note{unknown} / 7
		else
			string{unknown} := 0
		end if
	end if
	string{unknown} := min(string{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None}
	return (string{unknown})
end function

function subarticulation_event_get_free_index
	declare local idx : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local result : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	idx{unknown} := 0
	while(idx{unknown} < MAX_SUBARTICULATION_EVENTS0{unknown}) 
		if((subarticulation_event_list[idx{unknown}]{unknown} = - 1) and (subarticulation_event_last_used[idx{unknown}]{unknown} < (ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown} - lookahead{unknown})))
			result{unknown} := idx{unknown}
			idx{unknown} := MAX_SUBARTICULATION_EVENTS0{unknown}
		end if
		idx{unknown} := idx{unknown} + 1
	end while
	return (result{unknown})
end function

function subarticulation_event_fade_out(subarticulation_event_id : int, fade_time : int, stop_voice : int)
	if(subarticulation_event_is_event_active(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = TRUE{unknown})
		fade_out(subarticulation_event_get_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, fade_time{unknown} * 1000, stop_voice{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(subarticulation_octave_layer_is_event_active(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = TRUE{unknown})
			fade_out(subarticulation_octave_layer_get_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, fade_time{unknown} * 1000, stop_voice{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		if(subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
			fade_out(subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}, fade_time{unknown} * 1000, stop_voice{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		if(subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
			fade_out(subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}, fade_time{unknown} * 1000, stop_voice{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		if(stop_voice{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			subarticulation_event_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, - 1){UserDefined, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function subarticulation_group_count(subarticulation_id : int)
	declare local group_count : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
		group_count{unknown} := NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} * ((subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} * 3) + subarticulations_trans_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown})
	else
		group_count{unknown} := (NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} * subarticulations_interval_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * ((subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} * subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * (1 + subarticulations_release_group[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}))
	end if
	return (group_count{unknown})
end function

function subarticulation_purge(subarticulation_id : int, purge_state : int)
	for i{unknown} := 0 to subarticulation_group_count(subarticulation_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - 1
		purge_group((subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + i{unknown}) + TITLE_GROUP{unknown}, purge_state{unknown} * microphone_position_states[i{unknown} mod NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function subarticulation_play_note(instrument : int, keyswitch : int, subarticulation_idx : int, subarticulation_id : int, note : int, velocity : int, interval : int, rr : int, modulation : int, level : int, transpose : int, octave_layer : int, previous_note : int)
	declare local subarticulation_event_id : int := subarticulation_event_get_free_index{UserDefined, None} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local note_event : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local octave_event : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local transition_note_event : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local transition_octave_event : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local ii : int {Reuses: 0}
	if((subarticulation_event_id{unknown} # - 1) and (subarticulation_idx{unknown} # - 1))
		if((subarticulations_solo_states_any_active{unknown} = FALSE{unknown}) or (subarticulations_solo_states[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}))
			message("triggered subarticulation " & subarticulation_id{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} # SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
				note_event{unknown} := play_note(note{unknown} + transpose{unknown}, velocity{unknown}, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
				if(octave_layer{unknown} # 0)
					octave_event{unknown} := play_note((note{unknown} + transpose{unknown}) + (12 * octave_layer{unknown}), velocity{unknown}, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
				end if
				if((((subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_ONESHOT{unknown}) or (subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO_ATTACK{unknown})) or (subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_INTERVAL_SHORT{unknown})) or (subarticulation_id[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION{unknown}))
					message("previous_note: " & previous_note{unknown}){Builtin, None}
					if(previous_note{unknown} >= 0)
						if((articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[previous_note{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = instrument{unknown}) and (articulation_event_keyswitch[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[previous_note{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = keyswitch{unknown}))
							subarticulation_event_fade_out(previous_note{unknown}, 1000 - int((real(700){Builtin, None} * real(loaded_subarticulations_tightness[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}) / 100){Builtin, None}, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
						end if
					end if
				end if
				subarticulation_event_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, note_event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, octave_event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				subarticulation_event_set_event_mark(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, MARK_1{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				subarticulation_event_disallow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				for i{unknown} := 0 to subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} - 1
					for ii{unknown} := 0 to NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} - 1
						subarticulation_event_allow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, ((((subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + TITLE_GROUP{unknown}) + (((NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} * subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * (interval{unknown} * (1 + subarticulations_release_group[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown})))) + (((rr{unknown} * subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * (subarticulations_release_group[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + 1)) * NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown})) + ((i{unknown} * (subarticulations_release_group[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + 1)) * NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown})) + ii{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					end for
				end for
				subarticulation_event_change_vol(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, loaded_subarticulations_volume[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} * 1000, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION{unknown})
					repetition_engine_add(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				end if
			else
				declare local start_note : int {Reuses: 0}
				declare local end_note : int {Reuses: 0}
				declare local transition_note : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
				declare local transition_type : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
				declare local transition_dyn_layer : unknown := int((real(modulation{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 127){Builtin, None} / (128 / subarticulations_trans_num[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}) {Reuses: 0}
				declare local offset : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
				if(previous_note{unknown} >= 0)
					declare local transition_speed : real {Reuses: 0}
					if(loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
						transition_speed{unknown} := real(min(ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown} - subarticulation_event_last_used[previous_note{unknown}]{unknown}, 500){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / 500
						if(transition_speed{unknown} < 0.01)
							transition_speed{unknown} := 0
						end if
						transition_speed{unknown} := 1 - transition_speed{unknown}
					else
						transition_speed{unknown} := real(loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 100
					end if
					message("transition_speed: " & transition_speed{unknown}){Builtin, None}
					start_note{unknown} := subarticulation_event_actual_note[previous_note{unknown}]{unknown}
					end_note{unknown} := note{unknown} + transpose{unknown}
					if(((authoring_page_active{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (instrument{unknown} = 0)) and (subarticulation_idx{unknown} = 0))
						update_authoring_transition(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					end if
					if(abs(end_note{unknown} - start_note{unknown}){Builtin, None} <= MAX_INTERVAL{unknown})
						transition_note{unknown} := (end_note{unknown} * ne(ge(end_note{unknown} - start_note{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}) + (start_note{unknown} * ge(end_note{unknown} - start_note{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None})
						transition_type{unknown} := (1 + (abs(end_note{unknown} - start_note{unknown}){Builtin, None} * TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown})) + ((gt(end_note{unknown} - start_note{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} * 12) * TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown})
					else
						transition_note{unknown} := end_note{unknown}
						transition_type{unknown} := - TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}
					end if
					if(transition_type{unknown} >= 0)
						if(last_transitions_contains(instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_type{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = TRUE{unknown})
							offset{unknown} := 3
						else
							last_transitions_add_event(instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_type{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
						end if
						transition_note_event{unknown} := play_note(transition_note{unknown} + offset{unknown}, transition_type{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_zone_start{unknown}, legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None} * 1000, 0){Builtin, None}
						subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := transition_note_event{unknown}
						set_event_mark(transition_note_event{unknown}, MARK_1{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						change_tune(transition_note_event{unknown}, - offset{unknown} * 100000, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						if(octave_layer{unknown} # 0)
							transition_octave_event{unknown} := play_note((transition_note{unknown} + (12 * octave_layer{unknown})) + offset{unknown}, transition_type{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_zone_start{unknown}, legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown} + (12 * octave_layer{unknown}), transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, 0){Builtin, None}
							subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := transition_octave_event{unknown}
							set_event_mark(transition_octave_event{unknown}, MARK_1{unknown}){Builtin, None}
							change_tune(transition_octave_event{unknown}, - offset{unknown} * 100000, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						end if
						set_event_par_arr(transition_note_event{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, OFF{unknown}, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						if(transition_octave_event{unknown} # - 1)
							set_event_par_arr(transition_octave_event{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, OFF{unknown}, ALL_GROUPS{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						end if
						for i{unknown} := 0 to subarticulations_trans_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} - 1
							for ii{unknown} := 0 to NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} - 1
								set_event_par_arr(transition_note_event{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, ON{unknown}, (((subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + TITLE_GROUP{unknown}) + ((NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} * subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * 2)) + (i{unknown} * NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown})) + ii{unknown}){Builtin, None}
								if(transition_octave_event{unknown} # - 1)
									set_event_par_arr(transition_octave_event{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP{unknown}, ON{unknown}, (((subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + TITLE_GROUP{unknown}) + ((NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} * subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * 2)) + (i{unknown} * NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown})) + ii{unknown}){Builtin, None}
								end if
							end for
						end for
						set_event_par_arr(transition_note_event{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_fade_in_time{unknown}, legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, FADEIN_TRANS_SCRIPT_CC{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						set_event_par_arr(transition_note_event{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_fade_out_time{unknown}, legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, FADEOUT_TRANS_SCRIPT_CC{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						change_vol(transition_note_event{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_zone_volume{unknown}, legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None} + (loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} * 1000), TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}

							set_event_par_arr(transition_octave_event{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_fade_in_time{unknown}, legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown} + (12 * octave_layer{unknown}), transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, FADEIN_TRANS_SCRIPT_CC{unknown}){Builtin, None}
							set_event_par_arr(transition_octave_event{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_fade_out_time{unknown}, legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown} + (12 * octave_layer{unknown}), transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, FADEOUT_TRANS_SCRIPT_CC{unknown}){Builtin, None}
							change_vol(transition_octave_event{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_zone_volume{unknown}, legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None} + (loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} * 1000), TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						end if
						if((authoring_page_active{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (btn_play_transitions{unknown} = OFF{unknown}))
							fade_out(transition_note_event{unknown}, 1000, FALSE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
							if(transition_octave_event{unknown} # - 1)
								fade_out(transition_octave_event{unknown}, 1000, FALSE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
							end if
						end if
					end if
					if(subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[previous_note{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
						fade_out(subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[previous_note{unknown}]{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_sus_release_time{unknown}, legato_data_sus_release_time_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None} * 1000, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
					end if
					if((pressed_keys[subarticulation_event_note[previous_note{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = - 1) or (note_to_string(0, subarticulation_event_actual_note[previous_note{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = note_to_string(0, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}))
						subarticulation_event_fade_out(previous_note{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_sus_release_time{unknown}, legato_data_sus_release_time_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					else
						subarticulation_note_off(previous_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					end if
					if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
						declare local prev_release_event : int {Reuses: 0}
						prev_release_event{unknown} := release_per_string[instrument{unknown}, note_to_string(0, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
						if(prev_release_event{unknown} # - 1)
							fade_out(prev_release_event{unknown}, 2000000, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						end if

						if(prev_release_event{unknown} # - 1)
							fade_out(prev_release_event{unknown}, 2000000, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						end if

					end if
					note_event{unknown} := play_note(note{unknown}, velocity{unknown}, 800000, 0){Builtin, None}
					if(octave_layer{unknown} # 0)
						octave_event{unknown} := play_note((note{unknown} + transpose{unknown}) + (12 * octave_layer{unknown}), velocity{unknown}, 800000, 0){Builtin, None}
					end if
					subarticulation_event_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, note_event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, octave_event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
