					subarticulation_event_set_event_par_arr(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_sus_wait_time{unknown}, legato_data_sus_wait_time_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, WAIT_TIME_SCRIPT_CC{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					subarticulation_event_set_event_par_arr(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, get_legato_data(legato_data_sus_fade_in_time{unknown}, legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset{unknown}, instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, transition_note{unknown}, transition_dyn_layer{unknown}, transition_type{unknown} / TRANS_VELO_INTERVAL{unknown}, transition_speed{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, FADEIN_TIME_SCRIPT_CC{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					subarticulation_event_change_vol(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, loaded_subarticulations_volume[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} * 1000, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					if(transition_note_event{unknown} # - 1)
						change_vol(transition_note_event{unknown}, loaded_subarticulations_volume[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} * 1000, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						if(transition_octave_event{unknown} # - 1)
							change_vol(transition_octave_event{unknown}, loaded_subarticulations_volume[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} * 1000, TRUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						end if
					end if
					subarticulation_event_disallow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					for i{unknown} := 0 to subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} - 1
						for ii{unknown} := 0 to NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} - 1
							subarticulation_event_allow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, (((subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + TITLE_GROUP{unknown}) + (NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} * subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown})) + (i{unknown} * NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown})) + ii{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
						end for
					end for
					if((authoring_page_active{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (btn_play_sustain{unknown} = OFF{unknown}))
						fade_out(note_event{unknown}, 1000, FALSE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						if(octave_event{unknown} # - 1)
							fade_out(octave_event{unknown}, 1000, FALSE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						end if
					end if
				else
					note_event{unknown} := play_note(note{unknown}, velocity{unknown}, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
					if(octave_layer{unknown} # 0)
						octave_event{unknown} := play_note((note{unknown} + transpose{unknown}) + (12 * octave_layer{unknown}), velocity{unknown}, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
					end if
					subarticulation_event_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, note_event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, octave_event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					subarticulation_event_set_event_mark(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, MARK_1{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					subarticulation_event_disallow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					for i{unknown} := 0 to subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} - 1
						for ii{unknown} := 0 to NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} - 1
							subarticulation_event_allow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, ((subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + TITLE_GROUP{unknown}) + (i{unknown} * NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown})) + ii{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
						end for
					end for
					subarticulation_event_change_vol(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, loaded_subarticulations_volume[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown} * 1000, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					if((authoring_page_active{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (btn_play_sustain{unknown} = OFF{unknown}))
						fade_out(note_event{unknown}, 1000, FALSE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						if(octave_event{unknown} # - 1)
							fade_out(octave_event{unknown}, 1000, FALSE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
						end if
					end if
				end if
			end if
		end if
		subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := note{unknown}
		subarticulation_event_actual_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := note{unknown} + transpose{unknown}
		subarticulation_event_subarticulation[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := subarticulation_id{unknown}
		subarticulation_event_interval[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := interval{unknown}
		subarticulation_event_octave_layer[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := octave_layer{unknown}
		subarticulation_set_modulation(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, modulation{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		subarticulation_set_level(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, level{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := transition_note_event{unknown}
		subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := transition_octave_event{unknown}
		subarticulation_event_last_used[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}
		subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := subarticulation_idx{unknown}
	else
		message("WARNING: MAX_SUBARTICULATION_EVENTS reached"){Builtin, None}
	end if
	return (subarticulation_event_id{unknown})
end function

function subarticulation_note_off(subarticulation_event_id : int)
	if(subarticulation_event_is_event_active(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = TRUE{unknown})
		declare local subarticulation_id : int := subarticulation_event_subarticulation[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
		message("end subartevent " & subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if((subarticulations_release_time[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = 0) or ((ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown} - last_pressed[subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) < subarticulations_release_time[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}))
			note_off(subarticulation_event_get_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
			if(subarticulation_octave_layer_get_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None} # - 1)
				note_off(subarticulation_octave_layer_get_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
				declare local fade_time : unknown := 300 {Reuses: 0}
				subarticulation_event_fade_out(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, fade_time{unknown}, TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			end if
			if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION{unknown})
				repetition_engine_remove(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			end if
			if((subarticulations_release_group[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and ((authoring_page_active{unknown} = OFF{unknown}) or (btn_play_sustain{unknown} = ON{unknown})))
				declare local event : int := play_note(subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}, key_velocity[subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, 0, 0){Builtin, None} {Reuses: 0}
				declare local octave_event : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
				if(subarticulation_event_octave_layer[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} # 0)
					octave_event{unknown} := play_note(subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} + 12, key_velocity[subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, 0, 0){Builtin, None}
				end if
				subarticulation_event_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, octave_event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				subarticulation_event_disallow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
				declare local ii : int {Reuses: 0}
				for i{unknown} := 0 to subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} - 1
					for ii{unknown} := 0 to NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} - 1
						if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} # SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
							subarticulation_event_allow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, (((subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + TITLE_GROUP{unknown}) + (((NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} * subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) * (subarticulation_event_interval[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} * 2))) + (((i{unknown} * (subarticulations_release_group[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + 1)) + 1) * NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown})) + ii{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
						else
							subarticulation_event_allow_groups(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, (((subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + TITLE_GROUP{unknown}) + (NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown} * ((subarticulations_dynamic_layers[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} * 2) + subarticulations_trans_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}))) + (i{unknown} * NUM_MIC_POSITIONS{unknown})) + ii{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
						end if
					end for
				end for
				subarticulation_set_modulation(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, subarticulation_event_modulation[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				subarticulation_set_level(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, subarticulation_event_level[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
					release_per_string[articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, note_to_string(0, subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} := event{unknown}
					release_per_string[articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, note_to_string(0, subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} + 12){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} := octave_event{unknown}
				end if
			end if
		end if
		subarticulation_event_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, - 1){UserDefined, None}
		subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, - 1){UserDefined, None}
	end if
	subarticulation_event_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
	subarticulation_event_actual_note[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
	subarticulation_event_subarticulation[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
	subarticulation_event_modulation[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
	subarticulation_event_level[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
	subarticulation_event_interval[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := 0
	subarticulation_event_last_used[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}
	subarticulation_event_articulation_event[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
	subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
end function

function subarticulation_set_modulation(subarticulation_event_id : int, modulation : int)
	subarticulation_event_set_event_par_arr(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, modulation{unknown}, FROM_SCRIPT_MOD_ID{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	if(subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
		set_event_par_arr(subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, modulation{unknown}, FROM_SCRIPT_MOD_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
			set_event_par_arr(subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, modulation{unknown}, FROM_SCRIPT_MOD_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	subarticulation_event_modulation[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := modulation{unknown}
end function

function subarticulation_set_level(subarticulation_event_id : int, level : int)
	subarticulation_event_set_event_par_arr(subarticulation_event_id{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, level{unknown}, FROM_SCRIPT_LEV_ID{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	if(subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
		set_event_par_arr(subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, level{unknown}, FROM_SCRIPT_LEV_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
			set_event_par_arr(subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown}, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID{unknown}, level{unknown}, FROM_SCRIPT_LEV_ID{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	subarticulation_event_level[subarticulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := level{unknown}
end function

function subarticulation_reacts_to_modwheel(subarticulation_id : int)
	declare local result : unknown := FALSE{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	if(subarticulation_type_behavior_list[subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_id{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = 1)
		result{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
	end if
	return (result{unknown})
end function

function last_transitions_add_event(instrument : int, keyswitch : int, subarticulation_idx : int, note : int, transition_type : int)
	declare local idx : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local min : int := last_transitions_timecode[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, 0]{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local min_idx : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	if(transition_type{unknown} >= 0)
		for i{unknown} := 0 to 7
			if(last_transitions[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} = - 1)
				idx{unknown} := i{unknown}
				if(min{unknown} > last_transitions_timecode[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown})
					min{unknown} := last_transitions_timecode[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}
					min_idx{unknown} := i{unknown}
				end if
			end if
		end for
		if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
			last_transitions[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, idx{unknown}]{unknown} := (128 * transition_type{unknown}) + note{unknown}
			last_transitions_timecode[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, idx{unknown}]{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}
		else
			last_transitions[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, min_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := (128 * transition_type{unknown}) + note{unknown}
			last_transitions_timecode[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, min_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}
		end if
	end if
end function

function last_transitions_contains(instrument : int, keyswitch : int, subarticulation_idx : int, note : int, transition_type : int)
	declare local result : int := FALSE{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	call last_transitions_update{UserDefined, None}
	for i{unknown} := 0 to 7
		if(last_transitions[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} = ((128 * transition_type{unknown}) + note{unknown}))
			result{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
			last_transitions[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
		end if
	end for
	return (result{unknown})
end function

function last_transitions_update
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[_last_transitions{unknown}] - 1
		if(_last_transitions[i{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
			if(_last_transitions_timecode[i{unknown}]{unknown} < (ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown} - 2000))
				_last_transitions[i{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
			end if
		end if
	end for
end function

function articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(articulation_event_id : int, subarticulation : int)
	declare local result : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	if(articulation_event_id{unknown} >= 0)
		result{unknown} := articulation_event_list[articulation_event_id{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}
	end if
	return (result{unknown})
end function

function articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id(articulation_event_id : int, subarticulation : int, subarticulation_event_id : int)
	articulation_event_list[articulation_event_id{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := subarticulation_event_id{unknown}
end function

function articulation_event_clear(articulation_event_id : int)
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	if(articulation_event_id{unknown} # - 1)
		for i{unknown} := 0 to 4 - 1
			articulation_event_list[articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
		end for
		articulation_event_instrument[articulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
		articulation_event_keyswitch[articulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
		articulation_event_note[articulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
		articulation_event_timestamp[articulation_event_id{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
	end if
end function

function articulation_event_is_event_active(articulation_event_id : int)
	declare local is_active : int := FALSE{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	if(articulation_event_id{unknown} >= 0)
		for i{unknown} := 0 to 4 - 1
			if(articulation_event_list[articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
				if(subarticulation_event_is_event_active(articulation_event_list[articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = TRUE{unknown})
					is_active{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
				else
					if(articulation_event_list[articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} >= 0)
						articulation_event_clear(articulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					end if
				end if
			end if
		end for
	end if
	return (is_active{unknown})
end function

function articulation_event_get_free_index
	declare local next_free_idx : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local idx : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local is_free : int {Reuses: 0}
	while((next_free_idx{unknown} = - 1) and (idx{unknown} < MAX_ARTICULATION_EVENTS0{unknown})) 
		is_free{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
		for i{unknown} := 0 to 4 - 1
			if(articulation_event_list[idx{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
				is_free{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
			end if
		end for
		if((is_free{unknown} = TRUE{unknown}) and (event_list_contains(idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = FALSE{unknown}))
			next_free_idx{unknown} := idx{unknown}
		end if
		idx{unknown} := idx{unknown} + 1
	end while
	if(next_free_idx{unknown} = - 1)
		message("Articulation Event Buffer Full"){Builtin, None}
	end if
	return (next_free_idx{unknown})
end function

function articulations_on_note(instrument_slot : int, note : int, velocity : int, timing_offset : int)
	declare local ks : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local articulation_event_id : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local set_articulation_event_id : int := FALSE{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	for ks{unknown} := 0 to NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown} - 1
		if(keyswitch_states[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			articulation_event_id{unknown} := articulation_event_get_free_index{UserDefined, None}
			for i{unknown} := 0 to 4 - 1
				if(((loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1) and (note{unknown} >= subarticulations_range_lower[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown})) and (note{unknown} <= subarticulations_range_upper[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}))
					if(((subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_SUSTAINED{unknown}) or (subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_ONESHOT{unknown})) or (subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION{unknown}))
						if(event_list_get_articulation_event(instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = - 1)
							delay_buffer_add(articulation_event_id{unknown}, instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}, note{unknown}, velocity{unknown}, 0, ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}, ((lookahead{unknown} - subarticulations_start_offset[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) + timing_offset{unknown}) + humanize_by_ms(articulation_humanization[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
							if(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = - 1)
								articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id(articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}, EVENT_IN_PROGRESS{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
							end if
							set_articulation_event_id{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
						end if
					else
						if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO_ATTACK{unknown})
							message("active_notes: " & active_notes[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
							if(active_notes[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
								delay_buffer_add(articulation_event_id{unknown}, instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}, note{unknown}, velocity{unknown}, 0, ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}, ((lookahead{unknown} - subarticulations_start_offset[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) + timing_offset{unknown}) + humanize_by_ms(articulation_humanization[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
								if(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = - 1)
									articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id(articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}, EVENT_IN_PROGRESS{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
								end if
								set_articulation_event_id{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
							end if
						else
							if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
								if(event_list_get_articulation_event(instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = - 1)
									if(last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note_to_string(0, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} * allow_double_stops{unknown}]{unknown} = - 1)
										delay_buffer_add(articulation_event_id{unknown}, instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}, note{unknown}, velocity{unknown}, 0, ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}, ((lookahead{unknown} - subarticulations_start_offset[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) + timing_offset{unknown}) + humanize_by_ms(articulation_humanization[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note_to_string(0, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} * allow_double_stops{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
									else
										delay_buffer_add(articulation_event_id{unknown}, instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}, note{unknown}, velocity{unknown}, 0, ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}, (((lookahead{unknown} - subarticulations_start_offset[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) + timing_offset{unknown}) - (200 - get_legato_data(legato_data_trans_zone_start{unknown}, legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset{unknown}, instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}, note{unknown}, 0, transition_notes_to_type(note{unknown}, articulation_event_note[last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note_to_string(0, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} * allow_double_stops{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, 1 - (real(min(ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown} - articulation_event_timestamp[last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, 0]{unknown}]{unknown}, 500){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / 500)){UserDefined, None})) + humanize_by_ms(articulation_humanization[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note_to_string(0, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} * allow_double_stops{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
									end if
									if(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = - 1)
										articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id(articulation_event_id{unknown}, i{unknown}, EVENT_IN_PROGRESS{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
									end if
									set_articulation_event_id{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
									lbl_string_visualization[0]{unknown} -> picture_state := OFF{unknown}
									lbl_string_visualization[1]{unknown} -> picture_state := OFF{unknown}
									lbl_string_visualization[2]{unknown} -> picture_state := OFF{unknown}
									lbl_string_visualization[3]{unknown} -> picture_state := OFF{unknown}
									lbl_string_visualization[note_to_string(0, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} -> picture_state := ON{unknown}
								else
									message(note{unknown} & " note not cleared"){Builtin, None}
								end if
							else
								if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_INTERVAL_LONG{unknown})
									if(event_list_get_articulation_event(instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = - 1)
										delay_buffer_add(articulation_event_id{unknown}, instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}, note{unknown}, velocity{unknown}, 0, ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}, ((lookahead{unknown} - subarticulations_start_offset[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}) + timing_offset{unknown}) + humanize_by_ms(articulation_humanization[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, - 1){UserDefined, None}
									end if
								end if
							end if
						end if
					end if
				end if
			end for
			if(set_articulation_event_id{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
				event_list_add_articulation_event(instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}, articulation_event_id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				active_notes[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown} := active_notes[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}]{unknown} + 1
				message("set event id " & articulation_event_id{unknown} & " at " & instrument_slot{unknown} & ", " & ks{unknown} & ", " & note{unknown}){Builtin, None}
				last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note_to_string(0, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} * allow_double_stops{unknown}]{unknown} := articulation_event_id{unknown}
				last_articulation_event[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} := articulation_event_id{unknown}
			end if
		end if
	end for
end function

function articulations_note_off(instrument_slot : int, note : int)
	declare local ks : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local release_offset : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	for ks{unknown} := 0 to NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown} - 1
		if(event_list_get_articulation_event(instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} # - 1)
			for i{unknown} := 0 to 4 - 1
				if(loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
					if((subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_ONESHOT{unknown}) or (subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_INTERVAL_SHORT{unknown}))
						if(subarticulations_release_group[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
							release_offset{unknown} := 500
						end if
					end if
					delay_buffer_add(event_list_get_articulation_event(instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}, note{unknown}, - 1, 0, ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}, lookahead{unknown} + release_offset{unknown}, - 1){UserDefined, None}
				end if
			end for
			event_list_remove_articulation_event(instrument_slot{unknown}, ks{unknown}, note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		end if
	end for
end function

function articulations_compute_level(instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int, subarticulation : int)
	declare local subarticulation_modulation_strength : real := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local fade_in_start : int := loaded_subarticulations_start[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local fade_in_range : int := loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local fade_out_end : int := loaded_subarticulations_end[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local fade_out_range : int := loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, fade_in_start{unknown}, fade_out_end{unknown}){Builtin, None})
		subarticulation_modulation_strength{unknown} := 1
		if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, fade_in_start{unknown}, fade_in_start{unknown} + fade_in_range{unknown}){Builtin, None} and (fade_in_range{unknown} > 0))
			subarticulation_modulation_strength{unknown} := real(get_modulation_position(note{unknown}){UserDefined, None} - fade_in_start{unknown}){Builtin, None} / real(fade_in_range{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, fade_out_end{unknown} - fade_out_range{unknown}, fade_out_end{unknown}){Builtin, None} and (fade_out_range{unknown} > 0))
				subarticulation_modulation_strength{unknown} := real(fade_out_end{unknown} - get_modulation_position(note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / real(fade_out_range{unknown}){Builtin, None}
			end if
		end if
	end if
	return (int(1e+06 * ((real(articulations_compute_volume_curve(articulation_volume_min[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}, articulation_volume_max[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}, real(get_modulation_position(note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / 127, articulation_volume_curve[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / 127) * subarticulation_modulation_strength{unknown})){Builtin, None})
end function

function articulations_compute_volume_curve(min : int, max : int, x : real, curve : int)
	return (int(round(real(min{unknown}){Builtin, None} + (real(max{unknown} - min{unknown}){Builtin, None} * pow(x{unknown}, (real(curve{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 100) + 1){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function articulations_compute_modulation(instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int, subarticulation : int)
	return (int((1e+06 * (real(loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} + ((real(get_modulation_position(note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / 127) * real(loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} - loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}))) / 127){Builtin, None})
end function

function humanize_by_ms(time : int)
	return (random(- time{unknown} / 2, time{unknown} / 2){Builtin, None})
end function

function event_list_get_articulation_event(instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int)
	declare local result : unknown := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	if((((((instrument_slot{unknown} >= 0) and (instrument_slot{unknown} < NUM_INSTRUMENTS0{unknown})) and (keyswitch{unknown} >= 0)) and (keyswitch{unknown} < NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown})) and (note{unknown} >= 0)) and (note{unknown} < 128))
		result{unknown} := event_list[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown}
	end if
	return (result{unknown})
end function

function event_list_remove_articulation_event(instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int)
	if(((instrument_slot{unknown} # - 1) and (keyswitch{unknown} # - 1)) and (note{unknown} # - 1))
		if(event_list[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} >= 0)
			event_list[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
		end if
	end if
end function

function event_list_add_articulation_event(instrument_slot : int, keyswitch : int, note : int, event : int)
	event_list[instrument_slot{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} := event{unknown}
	articulation_event_instrument[event{unknown}]{unknown} := instrument_slot{unknown}
	articulation_event_keyswitch[event{unknown}]{unknown} := keyswitch{unknown}
	articulation_event_note[event{unknown}]{unknown} := note{unknown}
	articulation_event_timestamp[event{unknown}]{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}
end function

function event_list_contains(articulation_id : int)
	declare local result : int := FALSE{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	if(search[event_list{unknown}, articulation_id{unknown}] # - 1)
		result{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
	end if
	return (result{unknown})
end function

function delay_buffer_add(articulation_id : int, instrument : int, keyswitch : int, subarticulation : int, note : int, velo : int, interval : int, time : int, countdown : int, previous_note : int)
	declare local idx : int := search[delay_buffer{unknown}, - 1] {Reuses: 0}
	if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
		delay_buffer[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := articulation_id{unknown}
		delay_buffer_instrument[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := instrument{unknown}
		delay_buffer_keyswitch[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := keyswitch{unknown}
		delay_buffer_subarticulation[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := subarticulation{unknown}
		delay_buffer_note[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := note{unknown}
		delay_buffer_velo[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := velo{unknown}
		delay_buffer_interval[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := interval{unknown}
		delay_buffer_time[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := time{unknown}
		delay_buffer_countdown[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := countdown{unknown}
		delay_buffer_prev_note[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := previous_note{unknown}
		any_delay_event_queued{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
	else
		message("WARNING: Delay Buffer Full"){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function delay_buffer_execute
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local ii : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local articulation_event_is_empty : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local all_inactive : int := TRUE{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	if(any_delay_event_queued{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
		for i{unknown} := 0 to MAX_EVENTS0{unknown} - 1
			if(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
				delay_buffer_countdown[i{unknown}]{unknown} := delay_buffer_countdown[i{unknown}]{unknown} - LISTENER_RESOLUTION{unknown}
				if(delay_buffer_countdown[i{unknown}]{unknown} <= 0)
					if(delay_buffer_velo[i{unknown}]{unknown} >= 0)
						if(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None} < 0)
							declare local id : int := subarticulation_play_note(delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}, loaded_subarticulations[delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_note[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_velo[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_interval[i{unknown}]{unknown}, get_next_rr(delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_note[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, articulations_compute_modulation(delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_note[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, articulations_compute_level(delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_note[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, octave_shift[delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} * 12, octave_layer[delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(delay_buffer_prev_note[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None} {Reuses: 0}
							articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}, id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
							subarticulation_event_articulation_event[id{unknown}]{unknown} := delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}
						else
							message("articulation id " & delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown} & " already active"){Builtin, None}
						end if
					else
						if(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None} >= 0)
							if(subarticulation_event_articulation_event[articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown} = delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown})
								subarticulation_note_off(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}
							end if
							articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_subarticulation[i{unknown}]{unknown}, - 1){UserDefined, None}
							if(articulation_event_is_event_active(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = FALSE{unknown})
								message("clear " & delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
								active_notes[delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} := active_notes[delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} - 1
								if(delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown} = last_articulation_event[delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_note[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown})
									last_articulation_event[delay_buffer_instrument[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown}, delay_buffer_note[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
								end if
							end if
						end if
					end if
					delay_buffer[i{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
				end if
				all_inactive{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
			end if
		end for
		if(all_inactive{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			any_delay_event_queued{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
		end if
	end if
end function

function get_modulation_position(note : int)
	return (modulation_positions[note{unknown} * use_polyphonic_modulation{unknown}]{unknown})
end function

function set_modulation_position(note : int, value : int)
	modulation_positions[note{unknown} * use_polyphonic_modulation{unknown}]{unknown} := value{unknown}
end function

function cc_on_controller
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local e : int {Reuses: 0}
	for e : unknown in event_list{unknown}
		if(e{unknown} >= 0)
			for i{unknown} := 0 to 4 - 1
				if(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(e{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None} >= 0)
					if(subarticulation_reacts_to_modwheel(subarticulation_event_subarticulation[articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(e{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None} = TRUE{unknown})
						subarticulation_set_modulation(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(e{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, articulations_compute_modulation(articulation_event_instrument[e{unknown}]{unknown}, articulation_event_keyswitch[e{unknown}]{unknown}, articulation_event_note[e{unknown}]{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}
						subarticulation_set_level(articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id(e{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, articulations_compute_level(articulation_event_instrument[e{unknown}]{unknown}, articulation_event_keyswitch[e{unknown}]{unknown}, articulation_event_note[e{unknown}]{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}
					end if
				end if
			end for
		end if
	end for
end function

function is_in_note_selection(idx : int, num_pressed_notes : int, note_selection : int)
	declare local result : int := FALSE{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	select(note_selection{unknown})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_OFF{unknown}
		result{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST{unknown}
		result{unknown} := eq(idx{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST_TWO{unknown}
		result{unknown} := eq(idx{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} + eq(idx{unknown}, 1){UserDefined, None}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST_AND_LOWER_MIDDLE{unknown}
		result{unknown} := (eq(idx{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} + (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2){UserDefined, None} * le(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})) + (eq(idx{unknown}, (num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2) - 1){UserDefined, None} * gt(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST_AND_UPPER_MIDDLE{unknown}
		result{unknown} := (eq(idx{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} + (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2){UserDefined, None} * le(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})) + (eq(idx{unknown}, ((num_pressed_notes{unknown} - 2) / 2) + 1){UserDefined, None} * gt(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_MIDDLE{unknown}
		result{unknown} := eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2){UserDefined, None}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_MIDDLE_TWO{unknown}
		result{unknown} := (((eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2){UserDefined, None} * le(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None}) + (eq(idx{unknown}, (num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2) - 1){UserDefined, None} * gt(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})) + (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} + (1 / 2)){UserDefined, None} * le(num_pressed_notes{unknown} + 1, 3){UserDefined, None})) + (eq(idx{unknown}, (((num_pressed_notes{unknown} + 1) - 2) / 2) + 1){UserDefined, None} * gt(num_pressed_notes{unknown} + 1, 3){UserDefined, None})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWER_MIDDLE{unknown}
		result{unknown} := (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2){UserDefined, None} * le(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None}) + (eq(idx{unknown}, (num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2) - 1){UserDefined, None} * gt(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_UPPER_MIDDLE{unknown}
		result{unknown} := (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2){UserDefined, None} * le(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None}) + (eq(idx{unknown}, ((num_pressed_notes{unknown} - 2) / 2) + 1){UserDefined, None} * gt(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_HIGHEST{unknown}
		result{unknown} := eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} - 1){UserDefined, None}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_HIGHEST_TWO{unknown}
		result{unknown} := eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} - 1){UserDefined, None} + eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} - 2){UserDefined, None}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_HIGHEST_AND_LOWER_MIDDLE{unknown}
		result{unknown} := (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} - 1){UserDefined, None} + (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2){UserDefined, None} * le(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})) + (eq(idx{unknown}, (num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2) - 1){UserDefined, None} * gt(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_HIGHEST_AND_UPPER_MIDDLE{unknown}
		result{unknown} := (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} - 1){UserDefined, None} + (eq(idx{unknown}, num_pressed_notes{unknown} / 2){UserDefined, None} * le(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})) + (eq(idx{unknown}, ((num_pressed_notes{unknown} - 2) / 2) + 1){UserDefined, None} * gt(num_pressed_notes{unknown}, 3){UserDefined, None})
	case -2147483648 to 134217727
		result{unknown} := 0
	end select
	is_in_note_selection_boolean{unknown} := bool(result{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function update_selected_notes
	declare local ks : unknown {Reuses: 0}
	pressed_key_idx{unknown} := 0
	for i{unknown} := 0 to 127
		if(pressed_keys[i{unknown}]{unknown} > (ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown} - input_acceptance_time{unknown}))
			for inst{unknown} := 0 to NUM_INSTRUMENTS0{unknown} - 1
				is_in_note_selection(pressed_key_idx{unknown}, num_pressed_keys{unknown}, note_selections[inst{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				if(is_in_note_selection_boolean{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
					articulations_on_note(inst{unknown}, i{unknown}, key_velocity[i{unknown}]{unknown}, pressed_keys[i{unknown}]{unknown} - ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				else
					ks{unknown} := 0
					while(ks{unknown} < NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown}) 
						if(event_list_get_articulation_event(inst{unknown}, ks{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None} # - 1)
							articulations_note_off(inst{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
							ks{unknown} := NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown}
						end if
						inc(ks{unknown}){Builtin, None}
					end while
				end if
			end for
		else
			if(pressed_keys[i{unknown}]{unknown} > 0)
				for inst{unknown} := 0 to NUM_INSTRUMENTS0{unknown} - 1
					is_in_note_selection(pressed_key_idx{unknown}, num_pressed_keys{unknown}, note_selections[inst{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					if(is_in_note_selection_boolean{unknown} = FALSE{unknown})
						articulations_note_off(inst{unknown}, i{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
					end if
				end for
			end if
		end if
		if(pressed_keys[i{unknown}]{unknown} > 0)
			inc(pressed_key_idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
end function

function get_next_rr(instrument : int, keyswitch : int, subarticulation_idx : int, note : int)
	declare local rr : int {Reuses: 0}
	if(subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = 0)
		rr{unknown} := (rr_data_idx[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} + 1) mod subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}
	else
		if((ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown} - rr_data_time[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown}) > subarticulations_rrr_reset_time[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown})
			rr{unknown} := (rr_data_idx[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} + 1) mod subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}
		else
			rr{unknown} := max(subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, (rr_data_idx[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} + 1) mod subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		end if
		rr_data_time[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} := ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown}
	end if
	rr_data_idx[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, note{unknown}]{unknown} := rr{unknown}
	return (rr{unknown})
end function

function get_legato_data(legato_data_array : int[][][][][][], legato_offset_array : int[][][][][][], instrument : int, keyswitch : int, subarticulation_idx : int, note : int, layer : int, transition : int, offset : real)
	declare local result : int := - 1 {Reuses: 0}
	if((((((((instrument{unknown} >= 0) and (instrument{unknown} < NUM_INSTRUMENTS0{unknown})) and (subarticulation_idx{unknown} >= 0)) and (subarticulation_idx{unknown} < 4)) and (note{unknown} >= 0)) and (note{unknown} < 128)) and (layer{unknown} >= 0)) and (layer{unknown} < MAX_TRANSITION_DYN_LAYERS0{unknown}))
		if((transition{unknown} >= 0) and (transition{unknown} < MAX_TRANSITIONS_PER_NOTE0{unknown}))
			result{unknown} := legato_data_array[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, layer{unknown}, note{unknown}, transition{unknown}]{unknown} + int(offset{unknown} * real(legato_offset_array[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, layer{unknown}, note{unknown}, transition{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(transition{unknown} = - 1)
				result{unknown} := legato_data_array[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, layer{unknown}, 0, 0]{unknown} + int(offset{unknown} * real(legato_offset_array[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, layer{unknown}, 0, 0]{unknown}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
			end if
		end if
	end if
	return (result{unknown})
end function

	declare local transition_idx : int {Reuses: 0}
	for dyn_layer_idx{unknown} := 0 to MAX_TRANSITION_DYN_LAYERS0{unknown} - 1
		for note_idx{unknown} := 0 to 127
			for transition_idx{unknown} := 0 to MAX_TRANSITIONS_PER_NOTE0{unknown} - 1
				legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown}
				legato_data_sus_release_time[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown}
				legato_data_sus_wait_time[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time[dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown}
				legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time[dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown}
				legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time[dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown}

				legato_data_sus_wait_time_offset[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset[dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown}

	declare local dyn_layer_idx : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local note_idx : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local transition_idx : int {Reuses: 0}
	for dyn_layer_idx{unknown} := 0 to MAX_TRANSITION_DYN_LAYERS0{unknown} - 1
		for note_idx{unknown} := 0 to 127
			for transition_idx{unknown} := 0 to MAX_TRANSITIONS_PER_NOTE0{unknown} - 1
				legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown} := legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[instrument{unknown}, keyswitch{unknown}, subarticulation_idx{unknown}, dyn_layer_idx{unknown}, note_idx{unknown}, transition_idx{unknown}]{unknown}

function repetition_engine_listener
	for event : unknown in repetition_engine_subarticulation_events{unknown}
		if(event{unknown} # - 1)
			if(((ENGINE_UPTIME{unknown} - subarticulation_event_last_used[event{unknown}]{unknown}) mod repetition_interval_time{unknown}) < LISTENER_RESOLUTION{unknown})
				declare local subartid : int := subarticulation_event_subarticulation[event{unknown}]{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
				declare local id : int := subarticulation_play_note(articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[event{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, articulation_event_keyswitch[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[event{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[event{unknown}]{unknown}, subartid{unknown}, subarticulation_event_note[event{unknown}]{unknown}, get_modulation_position(subarticulation_event_note[event{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, subarticulation_event_interval[event{unknown}]{unknown}, get_next_rr(articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[event{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, articulation_event_keyswitch[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[event{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[event{unknown}]{unknown}, subarticulation_event_note[event{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}, subarticulation_event_modulation[event{unknown}]{unknown}, subarticulation_event_level[event{unknown}]{unknown}, octave_shift[articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[event{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} * 12, octave_layer[articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[event{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, event{unknown}){UserDefined, None} {Reuses: 0}
				articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id(subarticulation_event_articulation_event[event{unknown}]{unknown}, subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[event{unknown}]{unknown}, id{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				subarticulation_event_articulation_event[id{unknown}]{unknown} := subarticulation_event_articulation_event[event{unknown}]{unknown}
				subarticulation_note_off(event{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			end if
		end if
	end for
end function

function repetition_engine_add(subarticulation_event : int)
	declare local idx : int := search[repetition_engine_subarticulation_events{unknown}, - 1] {Reuses: 0}
	if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
		repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := subarticulation_event{unknown}
	else
		message("REACHED MAX_SUBARTICULATIONS_IN_REPETITION_ENGINE"){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function repetition_engine_remove(subarticulation_event : int)
	declare local idx : int := search[repetition_engine_subarticulation_events{unknown}, subarticulation_event{unknown}] {Reuses: 0}
	if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
		repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
	end if
end function

function reset_to_main_page
	btn_main_page{unknown} := ON{unknown}
	btn_editor_page{unknown} := OFF{unknown}
	btn_mixer_page{unknown} := OFF{unknown}
	call main_page_open{UserDefined, None}
	call editor_page_close{UserDefined, None}
	call mixer_page_close{UserDefined, None}
	show_keyswitches(TRUE{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function set_background_animation(frame : int)
	lbl_bg{unknown} -> picture := "bg_ani_" & ((frame{unknown} / 32) + 1)
	lbl_bg{unknown} -> picture_state := min(frame{unknown} mod 32, 30 + ne(eq(frame{unknown} / 32, 3){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function buffer_modwheel_animation(frame : int)
	next_modwheel_animation_frame{unknown} := frame{unknown}
end function

function set_key_colors
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	for i{unknown} := 0 to 127
		set_key_color(i{unknown}, KEY_COLOR_WHITE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if((i{unknown} >= 55) and (i{unknown} <= 96))
			set_key_color(i{unknown}, KEY_COLOR_BLUE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
end function

	authoring_close{UserDefined, None}
	pnl_main_page{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
end function

	pnl_main_page{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
end function
