	pnl_editor_page{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
end function

function editor_page_open
	pnl_editor_page{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
	sli_articulation_humanize{unknown} -> value := articulation_humanization[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}
	lbl_articulation_humanize{unknown} -> text := sli_articulation_humanize{unknown} & " ms"
	sli_articulation_release{unknown} -> value := articulation_release[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}
	lbl_articulation_release{unknown} -> text := sli_articulation_release{unknown} & " ms"
	call update_keyswitch_volume_curve{UserDefined, None}
	call update_subarticulation_selection{UserDefined, None}
	call update_keyswitch_settings{UserDefined, None}
	call update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, None}
	call update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, None}
	call update_dynamic_range_control{UserDefined, None}
end function

function update_keyswitch_settings
	txt_keyswitch_name{unknown} := articulation_names[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}
	call update_keyswitch_volume_curve{UserDefined, None}
end function

function update_subarticulation_selection
	ui_button_toggle_except(btn_edit_subarticulation_selection{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	if(loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
		btn_subarticulation_title{unknown} -> text := "    " & subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}
	else
		btn_subarticulation_title{unknown} -> text := "    Empty"
	end if
	btn_solo_subarticulation{unknown} -> value := subarticulations_solo_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}
	sli_subarticulation_volume{unknown} -> value := loaded_subarticulations_volume[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_volume{unknown} -> text := sli_subarticulation_volume{unknown} & " dB"
	sli_subarticulation_tightness{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_tightness{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	sli_subarticulation_vibrato{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_vibrato{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	sli_subarticulation_trans_volume{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	sli_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	btn_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_ONESHOT{unknown})
		sli_subarticulation_tightness{unknown} -> value := loaded_subarticulations_tightness[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_tightness{unknown} -> text := sli_subarticulation_tightness{unknown} & " %"
		sli_subarticulation_tightness{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_tightness{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
	end if
	if(((subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_SUSTAINED{unknown}) or (subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})) or (subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_INTERVAL_LONG{unknown}))
		sli_subarticulation_vibrato{unknown} -> value := loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_vibrato{unknown} -> text := sli_subarticulation_vibrato{unknown} & " %"
		sli_subarticulation_vibrato{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_vibrato{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
	end if
	if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
		sli_subarticulation_trans_volume{unknown} -> value := loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume{unknown} -> text := sli_subarticulation_trans_volume{unknown} & " dB"
		sli_subarticulation_trans_volume{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		sli_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} -> value := loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} -> text := sli_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} & " %"
		sli_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		btn_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} := loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}
		btn_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		if(btn_subarticulation_trans_speed{unknown} = ON{unknown})
			btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		end if
	end if
	call update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, None}
	call update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, None}
	call update_dynamic_range_control{UserDefined, None}
end function

function update_keyswitch_volume_curve
	sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min{unknown} -> value := articulation_volume_min[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}
	sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max{unknown} -> value := articulation_volume_max[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}
	sli_keyswitch_volume_curve{unknown} -> value := articulation_volume_curve[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown} * - 1
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{unknown}] - 1
		lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> height := articulations_compute_volume_curve(int((real(articulation_volume_min[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}, int((real(articulation_volume_max[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}, real(i{unknown}){Builtin, None} / real(num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{unknown}]){Builtin, None}, articulation_volume_curve[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
		lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> y := lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line{unknown} -> y - lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> height
	end for
end function

function update_keyswitch_volume_curve_cursor(modwheel : int)
	lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_cursor{unknown} -> x := (lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line{unknown} -> x - 5) + int(real(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None} * (real(modwheel{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127)){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_modwheel_assignment_control
	xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown} := real(loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} := real(loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} + loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown} := real(loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} - loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown} := real(loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_left{unknown} -> x := lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> x + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown} * real(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in{unknown} -> x := lbl_modwheel_assignment_left{unknown} -> x + int(- 200 + ((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown}) * real(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in{unknown} -> picture_state := int((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown}) * 200){Builtin, None}
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant{unknown} -> x := lbl_modwheel_assignment_left{unknown} -> x + int(round((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{unknown}) * real(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant{unknown} -> width := int((xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown} - xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{unknown}) * 200){Builtin, None}
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out{unknown} -> x := lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> x + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown} * real(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out{unknown} -> picture_state := int((xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown} - xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{unknown}) * 200){Builtin, None}
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_right{unknown} -> x := lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> x + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{unknown} * real(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_modwheel_assignment_cursor(modwheel : int)
	lbl_modwheel_assignment_cursor{unknown} -> x := (lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> x - 5) + int(real(lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None} * (real(modwheel{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127)){Builtin, None}
end function

function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
	for i{unknown} := 0 to 4 - 1
		lbl_center_circle[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
		lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
		lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
		if(loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
			lbl_center_circle[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
			lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
			lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
			if(i{unknown} = selected_subarticulation{unknown})
				lbl_center_circle[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> picture := "modwheel-circle-selected-" & i{unknown}
				lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> picture := "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & i{unknown}
				lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> picture := "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & i{unknown}
			else
				lbl_center_circle[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> picture := "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & i{unknown}
				lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> picture := "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & i{unknown}
				lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> picture := "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & i{unknown}
			end if
			lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> picture_state := loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}
			lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> picture_state := 127 - loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}
		end if
	end for
end function

function update_circle_modwheel_position(modwheel : int)
	lbl_center_circle_indicator{unknown} -> picture_state := modwheel{unknown} - 1
end function

function update_dynamic_range_control
	xy_dynamic_range[0]{unknown} := real(loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127
	xy_dynamic_range[2]{unknown} := real(loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 127
	lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{unknown} -> x := lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{unknown} -> x + int(xy_dynamic_range[0]{unknown} * real(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{unknown} -> x := lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{unknown} -> x + int(xy_dynamic_range[2]{unknown} * real(lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive{unknown} -> width){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
	lbl_dynamic_range_line{unknown} -> x := lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{unknown} -> x
	lbl_dynamic_range_line{unknown} -> width := lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{unknown} -> x - lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{unknown} -> x
	update_dynamic_range_cursor(get_modulation_position(0){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function update_dynamic_range_cursor(modwheel : int)
	lbl_dynamic_range_cursor{unknown} -> x := (lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{unknown} -> x - 5) + int((real(clamp(modwheel{unknown}, 1, 127){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / 127) * real(lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right{unknown} -> x - lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left{unknown} -> x){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
end function

function editor_update_modwheel_position(modwheel : int)
	update_dynamic_range_cursor(modwheel{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	update_circle_modwheel_position(modwheel{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	update_modwheel_assignment_cursor(modwheel{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	update_keyswitch_volume_curve_cursor(modwheel{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
end function

function center_circle_distance(x : real, y : real)
	declare local dx : unknown := x{unknown} - 0.5 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local dy : unknown := y{unknown} - 0.5 {Reuses: 0}
	return (sqrt((dx{unknown} * dx{unknown}) + (dy{unknown} * dy{unknown})){Builtin, None})
end function

function center_circle_angle(x : real, y : real)
	declare local dx : unknown := x{unknown} - 0.5 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local dy : unknown := y{unknown} - 0.5 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local cos_theta : unknown := dx{unknown} / sqrt((dx{unknown} * dx{unknown}) + (dy{unknown} * dy{unknown})){Builtin, None} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local angle : unknown := acos(cos_theta{unknown}){Builtin, None} {Reuses: 0}
	if(dy{unknown} < 0)
		angle{unknown} := (2 * NI_MATH_PI{unknown}) - angle{unknown}
	end if
	return (angle{unknown})
end function

function angle_to_value(angle : real, angle_min : real, angle_max : real)
	declare local new_angle : unknown := angle{unknown} + (NI_MATH_PI{unknown} / 2) {Reuses: 0}
	if(new_angle{unknown} > (NI_MATH_PI{unknown} * 2))
		new_angle{unknown} := new_angle{unknown} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{unknown})
	end if
	new_angle{unknown} := abs(new_angle{unknown} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{unknown})){Builtin, None}
	return (int((127 * (new_angle{unknown} - angle_min{unknown})) / (angle_max{unknown} - angle_min{unknown})){Builtin, None})
end function

function mixer_page_close
	pnl_mixer_page{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
end function

function mixer_page_open
	pnl_mixer_page{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
end function

function mixer_page_ui_controls(uiid : int)
	declare local idx : unknown := search[sli_mixer_channel_volume{unknown}, uiid{unknown}] {Reuses: 0}
	if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME{unknown}, sli_mixer_channel_volume[idx{unknown}]{unknown} -> value, - 1, - 1, NI_BUS_OFFSET{unknown} + idx{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(idx{unknown} = 4)
			set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME{unknown}, sli_mixer_channel_volume[idx{unknown}]{unknown} -> value, - 1, - 1, NI_BUS_OFFSET{unknown} + 5){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	idx{unknown} := search[btn_mixer_channel_enable{unknown}, uiid{unknown}]
	if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
		if(idx{unknown} < 4)
			microphone_position_states[idx{unknown}]{unknown} := btn_mixer_channel_enable[idx{unknown}]{unknown} -> value
		else
			microphone_position_states[idx{unknown} + mnu_mixer_bleed_channel{unknown}]{unknown} := btn_mixer_channel_enable[idx{unknown}]{unknown} -> value
			microphone_position_states[idx{unknown} + (1 - mnu_mixer_bleed_channel{unknown})]{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
		end if
		update_purge_microphone_positions{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function update_purge_microphone_positions
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local ii : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local iii : int {Reuses: 0}
	for i{unknown} := 0 to NUM_INSTRUMENTS0{unknown} - 1
		for ii{unknown} := 0 to NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown} - 1
			for iii{unknown} := 0 to 4 - 1
				if(loaded_subarticulations[i{unknown}, ii{unknown}, iii{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
					subarticulation_purge(loaded_subarticulations[i{unknown}, ii{unknown}, iii{unknown}]{unknown}, ON{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				end if
			end for
		end for
	end for
end function

function show_keyswitches(bool : int)
	if(bool{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
		pnl_keyswitches{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
	else
		pnl_keyswitches{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	end if
end function

function swi_keyswitch_ui_controls(uiid : unknown)
	declare local idx : unknown := search[swi_keyswitch{unknown}, uiid{unknown}] {Reuses: 0}
	if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
		if(swi_keyswitch[idx{unknown}]{unknown} -> key_shift = OFF{unknown})
			for i{unknown} := 0 to NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown} - 1
				keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} := OFF{unknown}
			end for
		end if
		keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, idx{unknown}]{unknown} := ON{unknown}
		selected_keyswitch{unknown} := idx{unknown}
		call update_keyswitch_selection{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function update_keyswitch_selection
	for i{unknown} := 0 to NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown} - 1
		swi_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}
		swi_keyswitch[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> text := articulation_names[selected_instrument{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}
		set_key_pressed((keyswitch_octave{unknown} * 12) + i{unknown}, keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end for
	call keyswitches_color_keys{UserDefined, None}
	if(pnl_editor_page{unknown} -> hide = HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown})
		call editor_page_open{UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function keyswitches_color_keys
	for i{unknown} := 0 to NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown} - 1
		set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{unknown} * 12) + i{unknown}, KEY_COLOR_RED{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		if(keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} = ON{unknown})
			set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{unknown} * 12) + i{unknown}, KEY_COLOR_ORANGE{unknown}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end for
end function

function keyswitches_on_note(note : int)
	declare local check_before : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local changed : int := FALSE{unknown} {Reuses: 0}
	if(in_range(note{unknown}, keyswitch_octave{unknown} * 12, ((keyswitch_octave{unknown} * 12) + NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown}) - 1){Builtin, None})
		for i{unknown} := 0 to NUM_KEYSWITCHES0{unknown} - 1
			check_before{unknown} := keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}
			keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} := KEY_DOWN[(keyswitch_octave{unknown} * 12) + i{unknown}]{unknown}
			if(check_before{unknown} # keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown})
				changed{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
			end if
			selected_keyswitch{unknown} := i{unknown}
		end for
		if(changed{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			call update_keyswitch_selection{UserDefined, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function subarticulation_browser_open
	pnl_subarticulation_browser{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
	if(loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
		subarticulation_browser_load_category(type_to_category[subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

function subarticulation_browser_close
	pnl_subarticulation_browser{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
end function

function gather_subarticulation_browser_entries
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local category_counter[7] : int[] := [0] {Reuses: 0}
	for i{unknown} := 0 to NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS0{unknown} - 1
		if(subarticulations_group_idx[i{unknown}]{unknown} # NI_NOT_FOUND{unknown})
			subarticulation_browser_entries[type_to_category[subarticulations_type[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}, category_counter[type_to_category[subarticulations_type[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} := i{unknown}
			category_counter[type_to_category[subarticulations_type[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} := category_counter[type_to_category[subarticulations_type[i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} + 1
		end if
	end for
end function

function subarticulation_browser_load_category(category : int)
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[btn_subarticulation_browser_selection{unknown}] - 1
		btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
		if(subarticulation_browser_entries[category{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} # - 1)
			btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> text := subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[subarticulation_browser_entries[category{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}
			if(subarticulation_browser_entries[category{unknown}, i{unknown}]{unknown} = loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown})
				btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := ON{unknown}
			else
				btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := OFF{unknown}
			end if
			btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		end if
	end for
	for i{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[btn_subarticulation_browser_category{unknown}] - 1
		if(i{unknown} = category{unknown})
			btn_subarticulation_browser_category[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := ON{unknown}
		else
			btn_subarticulation_browser_category[i{unknown}]{unknown} -> value := OFF{unknown}
		end if
	end for
	subarticulation_browser_active_category{unknown} := category{unknown}
end function

function subarticulation_browser_ui_controls(uiid : int)
	declare local idx : int {Reuses: 0}
	idx{unknown} := search[btn_subarticulation_browser_category{unknown}, uiid{unknown}]
	if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
		subarticulation_browser_load_category(idx{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
	end if
	idx{unknown} := search[btn_subarticulation_browser_selection{unknown}, uiid{unknown}]
	if(idx{unknown} # - 1)
		if(btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[idx{unknown}]{unknown} -> value = OFF{unknown})
			loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := - 1
			btn_subarticulation_title{unknown} -> text := "    Empty"
		else
			loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown} := subarticulation_browser_entries[subarticulation_browser_active_category{unknown}, idx{unknown}]{unknown}
			btn_subarticulation_title{unknown} -> text := "    " & subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}
			if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
				buffer_legato_data("leg" & loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}]{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
				move_legato_buffer_to_instrument(selected_instrument{unknown}, selected_keyswitch{unknown}, selected_subarticulation{unknown}){UserDefined, None}
			end if
		end if
	end if
end function

function set_font_types(uiid : int, font_array : int[])
	declare local v : int {Reuses: 0}
	for v{unknown} := 0 to num_elements[font_types{unknown}] - 1
		set_control_par(uiid{unknown}, font_types[v{unknown}]{unknown}, font_array[v{unknown}]{unknown}){Builtin, None}
	end for
end function

function settings_open
	pnl_settings{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
	btn_settings{unknown} -> value := ON{unknown}
end function

function settings_close
	pnl_settings{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	btn_settings{unknown} -> value := OFF{unknown}
end function

function authoring_open
	call find_loaded_legato{UserDefined, None}
	update_authoring_transition(60, 60, 0){UserDefined, None}
	pnl_authoring{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
end function

function authoring_close
	btn_show_authoring_tools{unknown} := OFF{unknown}
	pnl_authoring{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
	authoring_page_active{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
end function

function find_loaded_legato
	authoring_page_active{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
	if(loaded_subarticulations[0, 0, 0]{unknown} # - 1)
		if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[0, 0, 0]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_LEGATO{unknown})
			authoring_page_active{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
			lbl_authoring_legato_title{unknown} -> text := subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[0, 0, 0]{unknown}]{unknown}]{unknown} & " (" & loaded_subarticulations[0, 0, 0]{unknown} & ")"
		end if
	end if
end function

function update_authoring_transition(start_note : unknown, end_note : unknown, dynamic_layer : unknown)
	if(btn_authoring_follow{unknown} -> value = ON{unknown})
		vlue_authoring_start_note{unknown} -> value := start_note{unknown}
		vlue_authoring_end_note{unknown} -> value := end_note{unknown}
		mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown} -> value := dynamic_layer{unknown}
		if(abs(start_note{unknown} - end_note{unknown}){Builtin, None} <= 12)
			authoring_interval_valid{unknown} := TRUE{unknown}
			sli_sustain_release{unknown} -> value := legato_data_sus_release_time[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_trans_start{unknown} -> value := legato_data_trans_zone_start[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_trans_fadeIn{unknown} -> value := legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_trans_volume{unknown} -> value := legato_data_trans_zone_volume[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_trans_fadeOut{unknown} -> value := legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_sustain_wait{unknown} -> value := legato_data_sus_wait_time[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_sustain_fadeIn{unknown} -> value := legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_sustain_release_offset{unknown} -> value := legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_trans_start_offset{unknown} -> value := legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_trans_fadeIn_offset{unknown} -> value := legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_trans_volume_offset{unknown} -> value := legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_trans_fadeOut_offset{unknown} -> value := legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_sustain_wait_offset{unknown} -> value := legato_data_sus_wait_time_offset[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset{unknown} -> value := legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset[0, 0, 0, mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer{unknown}, start_note{unknown}, transition_notes_to_type(start_note{unknown}, end_note{unknown}){UserDefined, None}]{unknown}
			call update_authoring_labels{UserDefined, None}
		else
			authoring_interval_valid{unknown} := FALSE{unknown}
		end if
		if(authoring_interval_valid{unknown} = TRUE{unknown})
			btn_authoring_blocker{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
		else
			btn_authoring_blocker{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
		end if
	end if
end function

function update_authoring_labels
	lbl_sustain_release{unknown} -> text := sli_sustain_release{unknown} & " + " & sli_sustain_release_offset{unknown} & " ms"
	lbl_trans_start{unknown} -> text := sli_trans_start{unknown} & " + " & sli_trans_start_offset{unknown} & " ms"
	lbl_trans_fadeIn{unknown} -> text := int((real(sli_trans_fadeIn{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 750){Builtin, None} & " + " & int((real(sli_trans_fadeIn_offset{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 750){Builtin, None} & " ms"
	lbl_trans_volume{unknown} -> text := trim(real(sli_trans_volume{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1000, 2){UserDefined, None} & " + " & trim(real(sli_trans_volume_offset{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1000, 2){UserDefined, None} & " dB"
	lbl_trans_fadeOut{unknown} -> text := int((real(sli_trans_fadeOut{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 1000){Builtin, None} & " + " & int((real(sli_trans_fadeOut_offset{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 1000){Builtin, None} & " ms"
	lbl_sustain_wait{unknown} -> text := int((real(sli_sustain_wait{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " + " & int((real(sli_sustain_wait_offset{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " ms"
	lbl_sustain_fadeIn{unknown} -> text := int((real(sli_sustain_fadeIn{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " + " & int((real(sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset{unknown}){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " ms"
end function

function transition_notes_to_type(start_note : unknown, end_note : unknown)
	return (abs(end_note{unknown} - start_note{unknown}){Builtin, None} + (gt(end_note{unknown} - start_note{unknown}, 0){UserDefined, None} * 12))
end function

function credits_open
	pnl_credits{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_PART_NOTHING{unknown}
end function

function credits_close
	pnl_credits{unknown} -> hide := HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{unknown}
end function
